***владыка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:владыка.html>влады́ка</a> (6081)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">владꙑка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vladyka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">влади́ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vladíka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macedonian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Macedonian language">Macedonian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mk">владика</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vladika</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владыка.html>влады́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vladýka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владыка.html>влады́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владыка.html>влады́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владыка.html>влады́к</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владычица.html>влады́чица</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sovereign, lord, arbiter, overlord <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">judge without control</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Eastern Orthodoxy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> respectful</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bishop</li></ol>

<p><b>вла<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ды́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> согласовываться <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>частя́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>), 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владычество.html>влады́чество</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vladýčestvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владычество.html>влады́чества</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владычество.html>влады́чества</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:владычество.html>влады́честв</a></b>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влажный.html>вла́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlážnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)влажне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)влажне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>humid, moist, damp</li></ol>

<p><b>вла́ж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a/c'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>влажне́е, влажне́й.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-влаж-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***властвовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:властвовать.html>вла́ствовать</a> (11415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ствовать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:властвовать.html>вла́ствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlástvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to rule <i>(over)</i>, to hold sway <i>(over)</i>, to wield power <i>(over)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:властвовать.html>вла́ствовать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>собо́й</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">high-style</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlástvovatʹ</b> sobój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">control oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlastʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rule</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">er</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:властитель.html>власти́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlastítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:властитель.html>власти́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:властитель.html>власти́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:властитель.html>власти́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">власти́тельница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ruler, arbiter, sovereign
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:властитель.html>власти́тель</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дума.html>ду́м</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlastítelʹ</b> dum</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">a person of dominant influence</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:властный.html>вла́стный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlástnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:властный.html>вла́стно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlástno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>overpoweringly</li>
<li>in a domineering or peremptory manner</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:властный.html>вла́стный</a> (6543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:властный.html>вла́стный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlástnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)властне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)властне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>imperious, commanding, authoritative, masterful</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>вла́ст<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>властнее, властней.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-власт-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***власть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a> (319)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlastĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*volstь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волость.html>во́лость</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vólostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>вла́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>вла́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>authority, authorities, power</li>
<li>rule, regime</li>
<li>control</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> force <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">legal validity</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***влачить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:влачить.html>влачи́ть</a> (26986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">влачити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlačiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*volčiti</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волочить.html>волочи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voločítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влачить.html>влачи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlačítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic or figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drag, to draw</li></ol>

***влезать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:влезать.html>влеза́ть</a> (10281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vleztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влезать.html>влеза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlezátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get into (something, also figurative), to climb into, to scramble into
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влезать.html>влеза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>долги́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlezátʹ</b> v dolgí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">get into debts</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fit in, to go in</li>
<li>to meddle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влезать.html>влеза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlezátʹ</b> ne v svojó délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to poke one's nose into other people's affairs; to pry</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влезать.html>влеза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlezátʹ</b> v dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to worm oneself into smb.'s confidence (to get into somebody's soul)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>вле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>за́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-лез-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***влезть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a> (3541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vleztʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влезать.html>влеза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get into (something, also figurative), to climb into, to scramble into
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>вле́зет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skólʹko <b>vlézet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">as much as you like</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>долги́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vleztʹ</b> v dolgí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">get into debts</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fit in, to go in</li>
<li>to meddle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vleztʹ</b> ne v svojó délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to poke one's nose into other people's affairs; to pry</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>ду́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vleztʹ</b> v dúšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to worm oneself into smb.'s confidence (to get into somebody's soul)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влезть.html>влезть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влечь.html>влеко́мый</a></b>

***влепить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ть</a> (13318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепить.html>лепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">влепля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick in, to fasten in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slap <i>(on)</i>, to give a smack <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спине́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlepítʹ</b> komú-libo po spiné</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slap smb on the back</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:челюсть.html>че́люсть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlepítʹ</b> komú-libo v čéljustʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give smb a smack on the jaw</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:пуля.html>пу́лю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лоб.html>лоб</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlepítʹ</b> komú-libo púlju v lob</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put a bullet in smb's brain</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:пощечина.html>пощёчину</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlepítʹ</b> komú-libo poščóčinu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">give smb a slap in the face</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give, to deal/mete out <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlepítʹ</b> komú-libo dvójku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give smb a poor mark/grade</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьмы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>vlepíli</b> pjatʹ let tjurʹmý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was sent up for five years</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>вле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пи́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — влеплять, влепливать, <a href = vnd.unilang:лепить.html>лепи́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-леп-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влетать.html>влета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vletátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влететь.html>влете́ть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to fly into</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get into trouble

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:влететь.html>влете́ть</a> (6232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влететь.html>влете́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vletétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влетать.html>влета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly into</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run into <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to enter while running</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, to burst into</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get into trouble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:влететь.html>влете́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>vletélo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he got into trouble, he is in trouble</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***влечь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:влечь.html>влечь</a> (7893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">влѣщи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlěšti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*velťi</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волочь.html>воло́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">volóčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влечь.html>влечь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привлечь.html>привле́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завлечь.html>завле́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увлечь.html>увле́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повлечь.html>повле́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to attract, to draw, to pull, to haul</li>
<li>to entail, to bring about
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">нея́вка <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:избирательный.html>избира́тельные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:участок.html>уча́стки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уважительный.html>уважи́тельных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причина.html>причи́н</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:влечь.html>влечёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>собо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штраф</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> Люксембурге</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nejávka na izbirátelʹnyje učástki bez uvažítelʹnyx pričín <b>vlečót</b> za sobój štraf v Ljuksemburge</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Unless a valid reason is given, not attending the polling stations <b>entails</b> a fine in Luxembourg</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повлечь.html>повле́чь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">povléčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вливать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вливать.html>влива́ть</a> (20358)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влить.html>влить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vlitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вливать.html>влива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vlivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влить.html>влить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pour in, to instil, to pour <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вливать.html>влива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бочок.html>бо́чку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlivátʹ</b> vódu v bóčku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pour water into a barrel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вливать.html>влива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:капля.html>ка́пле</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlivátʹ</b> po káple</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to instil (put in) by drops; put in drop by drop</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to instil <i>(in, into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вливать.html>влива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужество.html>му́жество</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>реши́мость</a>) (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vlivátʹ</b> múžestvo (rešímostʹ) (v)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">instil courage (resolution) (in, into)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>.
